msg:I recently had the pleasure of staying at Shangrila, and I must say it was a fantastic experience! From the moment we arrived, the staff went above and beyond to make our stay memorable.
Highlights of Our Stay:

Exceptional Service:¬†The staff were incredibly friendly and attentive. We had a special request for a small birthday setup for my husband, and they exceeded our expectations. The room was beautifully decorated with balloons and a birthday cake, which made the celebration extra special.

Comfortable Accommodation:¬†The room was spacious, clean, and well-appointed with all the amenities we needed. The beds were comfortable, and we had a great night's sleep of our stay.

Excellent Dining:¬†The hotel's restaurant offered a wide variety of delicious dishes. We especially enjoyed the breakfast buffet, which had something for everyone, including picky eaters!

Areas for Improvement:
While our stay was wonderful, one area where the hotel could improve is in making the facilities more child-friendly. It would be fantastic to have an indoor playground and a dedicated kids' pool. These additions would make the hotel even more appealing for families with young children.

Overall, Shangrila provided an excellent experience with top-notch service and amenities. We will definitely consider staying here again in the future and look forward to seeing any new child-friendly additions they might make!

Hygiene:

Cost performance:
The price on May Day is 1.7k, which is OK.

msg:A hotel with an excellent location for shopping, leisure and entertainment~
Within 300-400 meters walking distance of Qiantan Shangri-La, there are Qiantan Taikoo Li, Qiantan Jingyao, and Qiantan 31 Lehui. It can be said that it is very convenient to eat, relax and go shopping, especially Taikoo Li Qiantan is bordered by the hotel. Whether you walk to Taikoo Li from the parking lot or open air, you don‚Äôt have to worry about rain. Below Taikoo Li is the Oriental Sports Center Subway Station, where lines 6, 8, and 11 intersect. I saw some hotel guests coming back from Disney, and Line 11 can be reached in half an hour, which can be said to be very convenient.
Next to the location, the second best thing is the service. From the checkin lady to the hallway waiter, the little brother in the hall, the breakfast waiter, the afternoon tea lady, the room service lady, the gym receptionist, and the storage staff are all very polite, smiling, and have a gentle and friendly attitude. All the proposed service needs are arranged in place, such as "okay", "yes", "no problem" and "should" are all on the lips, which makes people feel very comfortable. This is still the quality of service during 5.1.
The environment and room layout of the hotel are not the best among five-star hotels. They are not luxurious but warm and comfortable. The ultra-luxury double room is 45m2. Although it is not as large as other rooms of the same level, it is still sufficient. However, there are no scales, umbrellas, coffee machines in the room, no Bluetooth speakers in the parents' room (the type shared with me), and no preset razors in the toiletries (it is commendable that they will be delivered immediately after talking to room service), These items may be deduction items for which I did not score all 5 points, which can be used as a reference for other guests.
In addition, the hotel's gym has a large area and abundant fitness equipment, which can be said to be the most in Shanghai, and the gym can be rated as 6 stars. Of course, the swimming pool is also very good, you can try it~
Breakfast is divided into Chinese food and Western food. For Chinese food, there are special stalls for pancakes and fruits, as well as wonton noodle stalls, bean curd/salty soy milk stalls, and a wide variety of dishes (especially fruits, more than a dozen kinds every day), and the taste is worthless. It is still better than attentive service.
